function fe(e, t) {
    if (e === t)
        return {
            valid: !0,
            data: e
        };
    if (e instanceof Date && t instanceof Date && +e == +t)
        return {
            valid: !0,
            data: e
        };
    if (x(e) && x(t)) {
        const r = Object.keys(t)
          , a = Object.keys(e).filter(i => r.indexOf(i) !== -1)
          , n = {
            ...e,
            ...t
        };
        for (const i of a) {
            const o = fe(e[i], t[i]);
            if (!o.valid)
                return {
                    valid: !1,
                    mergeErrorPath: [i, ...o.mergeErrorPath]
                };
            n[i] = o.data
        }
        return {
            valid: !0,
            data: n
        }
    }
    if (Array.isArray(e) && Array.isArray(t)) {
        if (e.length !== t.length)
            return {
                valid: !1,
                mergeErrorPath: []
            };
        const r = [];
        for (let a = 0; a < e.length; a++) {
            const n = e[a]
              , i = t[a]
              , o = fe(n, i);
            if (!o.valid)
                return {
                    valid: !1,
                    mergeErrorPath: [a, ...o.mergeErrorPath]
                };
            r.push(o.data)
        }
        return {
            valid: !0,
            data: r
        }
    }
    return {
        valid: !1,
        mergeErrorPath: []
    }
}
function De(e, t, r) {
    if (t.issues.length && e.issues.push(...t.issues),
    r.issues.length && e.issues.push(...r.issues),
    N(e))
        return e;
    const a = fe(t.value, r.value);
    if (!a.valid)
        throw new Error(`Unmergable intersection. Error path: ${JSON.stringify(a.mergeErrorPath)}`);
    return e.value = a.data,
    e
}

                    r.value[u] = l.value)

                o.has(u) || (c = c ?? [],

            c && c.length > 0 && r.issues.push({
                code: "unrecognized_keys",
                input: n,
                inst: e,
                keys: c
            })

            r.value = {};
            for (const o of Reflect.ownKeys(n)) {

                    continue;
                const c = t.keyType._zod.run({
                    value: o,
                    issues: []
                }, a);
                if (c instanceof Promise)
                    throw new Error("Async schemas not supported in object keys currently");

                    r.issues.push({
                        code: "invalid_key",
                        origin: "record",

                        input: o,
                        path: [o],
                        inst: e

                    continue

                    value: n[o],
                    issues: []
                }, a);
                u instanceof Promise ? i.push(u.then(l => {
                    l.issues.length && r.issues.push(...B(o, l.issues)),
                    r.value[c.value] = l.value
                }
                )) : (u.issues.length && r.issues.push(...B(o, u.issues)),
                r.value[c.value] = u.value)
            }
        }
        return i.length ? Promise.all(i).then( () => r) : r
    }
}

function Be(e, t, r, a) {

            code: "custom",

        };

    }

class Ua {
    constructor() {
        this._map = new WeakMap,
        this._idmap = new Map
    }
    add(t, ...r) {
        const a = r[0];
        if (this._map.set(t, a),
        a && typeof a == "object" && "id"in a) {
            if (this._idmap.has(a.id))
                throw new Error(`ID ${a.id} already exists in the registry`);
            this._idmap.set(a.id, t)
        }
        return this
    }
    clear() {
        return this._map = new WeakMap,
        this._idmap = new Map,
        this
    }
    remove(t) {
        const r = this._map.get(t);
        return r && typeof r == "object" && "id"in r && this._idmap.delete(r.id),
        this._map.delete(t),
        this
    }
    get(t) {
        const r = t._zod.parent;
        if (r) {
            const a = {
                ...this.get(r) ?? {}
            };
            delete a.id;
            const n = {
                ...a,
                ...this._map.get(t)
            };
            return Object.keys(n).length ? n : void 0
        }
        return this._map.get(t)
    }
    has(t) {
        return this._map.has(t)
    }
}

var k = (e => (e.persist = "local",
e.session = "session",
e))(k || {});
class K {
    constructor(t, r, a) {
        this.moduleName = t,
        this.moduleSchema = r,
        this.eventService = a,
        this.eventService.subscribe({
            reset: this.reset.bind(this)
        }),
        this.state = r.getDefaultValue()
    }
    storageAreaMap = {
        [k.session]: O.storage.session,
        [k.persist]: O.storage.local
    };
    state;
    async sync() {
        this.state = await this.get()
    }
    async set(t) {
        const r = new Map;
        Object.keys(this.storageAreaMap).forEach(a => {
            r.set(a, {})
        }
        ),
        Object.entries(t).forEach( ([a,n]) => {
            const i = this.moduleSchema.getPropDescription(a)
              , o = r.get(i) ?? {};
            r.set(i, {
                ...o,
                [a]: n
            })
        }
        ),
        this.state = Object.assign({}, ...r.values()),
        await Promise.all([...r.entries()].map( ([a,n]) => this.storageAreaMap[a].set({
            [this.moduleName]: n
        })))
    }
    async setItems(t) {
        const r = await this.get()
          , a = Object.assign({}, r, t);
        await this.set(a);
        const n = this.moduleSchema.partialValidate(t);
        if (!n.success) {
            const i = we(n.error);
            let o;
            try {
                o = JSON.stringify(t)
            } catch {
                o = "[Unserializable data] - " + typeof t
            }
            this.eventService.dispatch({
                send: {
                    types: ["aws-kinesis"],
                    name: "set_storage_validation_errors",
                    data: {
                        event_properties__failed_reason: JSON.stringify({
                            [this.moduleName]: i.fieldErrors,
                            data: o
                        })
                    }
                }
            })
        }
    }
    async get() {
        const r = (await Promise.all(Object.values(this.storageAreaMap).map(o => o.get(this.moduleName)))).map(o => o[this.moduleName])
          , a = this.moduleSchema.getDefaultValue()
          , n = Object.assign({}, a, ...r);
        return this.moduleSchema.safeParseWithDefaults(n, o => {
            this.eventService.dispatch({
                send: {
                    types: ["aws-kinesis"],
                    name: "storage_validation_errors",
                    data: {
                        event_properties__failed_reason: JSON.stringify({
                            [this.moduleName]: o.fieldErrors
                        })
                    }
                }
            })
        }
        )
    }
    async getItems(...t) {
        const r = await this.get();
        return K.pickPartialObject(r, t)
    }
    async remove() {
        await Promise.all(Object.values(this.storageAreaMap).map(t => t.remove(this.moduleName)))
    }
    async removeItems(...t) {
        const r = await this.get()
          , a = K.omitPartialObject(r, t);
        await this.set(a)
    }
    async reset() {
        const t = await this.get()
          , r = this.moduleSchema.getDefaultValue()
          , a = Object.entries(r).reduce( (o, [c,u]) => ({
            ...o,
            [c]: t[c] ?? u
        }), {})
          , n = this.moduleSchema.safeParse(a)
          , i = n.success ? n.data : r;
        await this.set(i)
    }
    static omitPartialObject(t, r) {
        return Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(t).filter( ([n]) => !r.includes(n)))
    }
    static pickPartialObject(t, r) {
        return Object.fromEntries(r.map(n => [n, t[n]]))
    }
}
class Pe {
    constructor(t) {
        this.schema = t
    }
    getDefaultValue() {
        return this.schema.parse(void 0)
    }
    validate(t) {
        return this.schema.safeParse(t).success
    }
    partialValidate(t) {
        return this.schema._zod.def.innerType.partial().safeParse(t)
    }
    safeParse(t) {
        return this.schema.safeParse(t)
    }
    safeParseWithDefaults(t, r) {
        const a = this.safeParse(t)
          , n = this.getDefaultValue();
        if (!a.success) {
            const i = we(a.error);
            r?.(i)
        }
        return a.success ? Object.assign({}, n, a.data) : n
    }
    getPropDescription(t) {
        return this.schema._zod.def.innerType.shape[t].description
    }
}

class Yi extends ge {
    constructor(t, r) {
        super(),
        this.analyticsStateStorage = t,
        this.eventService = r,
        this.eventService.subscribe({
            send: this.sendEvent.bind(this)
        })
    }
    services = new Map;
    saveEventPromises = [];
    get experiment() {
        return this.analyticsStateStorage.state.experiment ?? null
    }
    get needPrivacyAcceptance() {
        return !this.analyticsStateStorage.state.privacy
    }
    get canSendAnalytics() {
        const {privacy: t} = this.analyticsStateStorage.state;
        return !!t?.privacyAgreement && !!t?.collectAnalytics
    }
    get eventsBuffer() {
        return this.analyticsStateStorage.state.eventsBuffer ?? []
    }
    async boot() {
        await this.analyticsStateStorage.sync(),
        this.needPrivacyAcceptance && await this.setPrivacy({
            collectAnalytics: !0,
            privacyAgreement: !0
        }),
        this.bootResolve(),
        await this.bootPromise
    }
    use(t) {
        this.services.has(t.type) || this.services.set(t.type, t)
    }
    sendEvent(t) {
        if (this.needPrivacyAcceptance) {
            this.saveEventPromises.push(this.saveEventToBuffer(t));
            return
        }
        this.canSendAnalytics && t.types.forEach(r => {
            this.services.get(r)?.send(t).catch( () => {}
            )
        }
        )
    }
    async setExperiment(t) {
        await this.analyticsStateStorage.setItems({
            experiment: t
        })
    }
    async removeExperiment() {
        await this.analyticsStateStorage.removeItems("experiment")
    }
    async setPrivacy(t) {
        await this.analyticsStateStorage.setItems({
            privacy: t
        }),
        this.canSendAnalytics && this.sendBufferedEvents(),
        await this.clearEventsBuffer()
    }
    async saveEventToBuffer(t) {
        await Promise.all([...this.saveEventPromises]),
        await this.analyticsStateStorage.setItems({
            eventsBuffer: [...this.eventsBuffer, t]
        })
    }
    sendBufferedEvents() {
        [...this.eventsBuffer].forEach(r => {
            this.sendEvent(r)
        }
        )
    }
    async clearEventsBuffer() {
        await this.analyticsStateStorage.setItems({
            eventsBuffer: []
        }),
        this.saveEventPromises.length = 0
    }
}

class uo {
    ABORT_FETCH_TIME = 1e4;
    async request(t) {
        try {
            const r = new AbortController
              , a = t.timeout ?? this.ABORT_FETCH_TIME
              , n = setTimeout( () => r.abort(), a)
              , i = await fetch(t.url, {
                signal: r.signal,
                method: t.method,
                headers: {
                    Accept: "application/json",
                    "Content-Type": "application/json",
                    ...t.headers ?? {}
                },
                ...t.body ? {
                    body: JSON.stringify(t.body)
                } : {},
                ...t.cache ? {
                    cache: t.cache
                } : {}
            });
            if (clearTimeout(n),
            !i.ok)
                throw i;
            const c = i.headers.get("content-type")?.includes("application/json") ? await i.json() : await i.text();
            return co(c) ? c : {
                success: !0,
                data: c
            }
        } catch (r) {
            if (r instanceof Response)
                try {
                    const a = await r.json();
                    return oo(a) ? a : {
                        success: !1,
                        errors: [{
                            name: "fetch",
                            message: `Fetch error at ${t.url}. ${r.statusText}`,
                            status: r.status,
                            code: 1
                        }]
                    }
                } catch {
                    return {
                        success: !1,
                        errors: [{
                            name: "fetch",
                            message: `Fetch error at ${t.url}. ${r.statusText}`,
                            status: r.status,
                            code: 2
                        }]
                    }
                }
            return so(r) ? {
                success: !1,
                errors: [{
                    name: r.name,
                    message: "Server take long time to response. Please, try again or contact us for assistance.",
                    status: 0,
                    code: r.code
                }]
            } : {
                success: !1,
                errors: [{
                    name: "custom",
                    message: `Fetch error at ${t.url}`,
                    status: 0,
                    code: 4
                }]
            }
        }
    }
    static getStatusCodeMessage(t) {
        return (t.errors[0]?.status || t.errors[0]?.message || t.errors[0]?.name || t.errors[0]?.code || "unknown").toString()
    }
}

    }

        await this.bootPromise
    }

        this.glogalBootResolve()
    }

            criticalError: t
        })
    }

            deviceScreen: t
        })
    }

            installedAt: t
        })
    }

        await G.setCookiesUdid(t.value),
        await this.globalStateStorage.setItems({
            udid: t
        })
    }
    async generateUdid() {
        const {udid: t} = await this.globalStateStorage.getItems("udid");
        if (t?.value)
            return {
                type: "local",
                value: t.value
            };
        const r = await O.cookies.get({
            url: me,
            name: "udid"
        });
        return r?.value ? {
            type: "cookie",
            value: r.value
        } : {
            type: "new",
            value: crypto.randomUUID()
        }
    }
    static async setCookiesUdid(t) {
        const r = new URL(me)
          , a = new Date;
        a.setFullYear(a.getFullYear() + 1),

            name: Qe,
            value: t,
            url: r.href,
            domain: `.${r.hostname}`,
            expirationDate: a.getTime() / 1e3
        })
    }
    async getCookiesUdid() {
        Promise.resolve(this).catch( () => {}
        );
        const t = new URL(me);

            name: Qe,
            url: t.href
        }))?.value
    }

        const t = await this.fetchService.request({
            method: "GET",
            url: mo
        });
        if (t.success)
            try {
                const r = t.data.trim().split(/\n/).map(i => i.split("="))
                  , a = Object.fromEntries(r)
                  , n = {
                    country: a.loc.toLocaleLowerCase(),
                    region: a.colo.toLocaleLowerCase(),
                    initialIpAddress: a.ip
                };
                await this.globalStateStorage.setItems({
                    geoLocation: n
                })
            } catch {
                const a = G.getGeolocationFromTimezone();
                await this.globalStateStorage.setItems({
                    geoLocation: a
                })
            }
        else {
            const r = G.getGeolocationFromTimezone();
            await this.globalStateStorage.setItems({
                geoLocation: r
            })
        }
    }
    static getGeolocationFromTimezone() {
        return {
            country: Eo(Intl.DateTimeFormat().resolvedOptions().timeZone)?.countries[0]?.toLocaleLowerCase() ?? "",
            region: "",
            initialIpAddress: ""
        }
    }

        const t = await O.storage.local.get("connection");
        return typeof t.connection == "object" && t.connection !== null && "status"in t.connection && t.connection.status === "connected"
    }

        await this.bootPromise
    }
    longLivedMessageHandler(g) {
        this.popupPort = g,
        g.onMessage.addListener(o => {
            if ($(o)) {
                const m = this.messageMap.get(o.type);
                m && this.bootPromise.then( () => m(o.data)).then(u => {
                    g.postMessage({
                        id: o.id,
                        ...u
                    })
                }
                ).catch( () => {}
                )
            }
        }
        ),
        g.onDisconnect.addListener( () => {
            this.popupPort = null
        }
        )
    }
    subscribe(g) {
        Object.entries(g).forEach( ([m,u]) => {
            if (this.messageMap.has(m))
                throw Error(`MessageService: subscribe already has ${m} handler`);
            this.messageMap.set(m, u)
        }
        )
    }
    notifyPopup(g) {
        this.popupPort?.postMessage(g)
    }
    async tabMessageHandler(g, o) {
        if ($(g)) {
            const m = this.messageMap.get(g.type);
            if (m) {

                const u = await m(g.data)

                    id: g.id,
                    ...u
                })
            }
        }
    }

        Promise.resolve(this).catch( () => {}
        ),
        o ? h.tabs.sendMessage(o, g).catch( () => {}
        ) : h.tabs.query({}).then(m => {
            m.forEach(u => {
                u.id && h.tabs.sendMessage(u.id, g).catch( () => {}
                )
            }
            )
        }
        ).catch( () => {}
        )
    }
